 63.660 PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> SELECT * WHERE {  ?airport a <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/Airport>; rdfs:label ?name. {?airport <http://dbpedia.org/property/iata> 'CVG'@en.} UNION  {?airport <http://dbpedia.org/ontology/iataLocationIdentifier> 'CVG'@en. } OPTIONAL { ?airport foaf:homepage ?airport_home. } OPTIONAL { ?airport rdfs:label ?name. } OPTIONAL { ?airport <http://dbpedia.org/property/nativename> ?airport_name.} FILTER ( !bound(?name) || langMatches( lang(?name), 'fr') )}
